33529: #if !defined(WINCE)
57093: static PRBool
62477: HasRegistryKey(HKEY aRoot, PRUnichar* aName)
57093: {
57093:   HKEY key;
57093:   LONG result = ::RegOpenKeyExW(aRoot, aName, 0, KEY_READ, &key);
57093:   if (result != ERROR_SUCCESS)
57093:     return PR_FALSE;
57093:   ::RegCloseKey(key);
57093:   return PR_TRUE;
57093: }
57093: 
62477: /**
62477:  * Gets the value of a string-typed registry value.
62477:  *
62477:  * @param aRoot The registry root to search in.
62477:  * @param aKeyName The name of the registry key to open.
62477:  * @param aValueName The name of the registry value in the specified key whose
62477:  *   value is to be retrieved.  Can be null, to retrieve the key's unnamed/
62477:  *   default value.
62477:  * @param aBuffer The buffer into which to store the string value.  Can be null,
62477:  *   in which case the return value indicates just whether the value exists.
62477:  * @param aBufferLength The size of aBuffer, in bytes.
62477:  * @return Whether the value exists and is a string.
62477:  */
57093: static PRBool
62477: GetRegistryKey(HKEY aRoot, PRUnichar* aKeyName, PRUnichar* aValueName, PRUnichar* aBuffer, DWORD aBufferLength)
62477: {
62477:   if (!aKeyName) {
62477:     return PR_FALSE;
62477:   }
62477: 
57093:   HKEY key;
62477:   LONG result = ::RegOpenKeyExW(aRoot, aKeyName, NULL, KEY_READ, &key);
57093:   if (result != ERROR_SUCCESS)
57093:     return PR_FALSE;
57093:   DWORD type;
62477:   result = ::RegQueryValueExW(key, aValueName, NULL, &type, (BYTE*) aBuffer, &aBufferLength);
57093:   ::RegCloseKey(key);
57093:   if (result != ERROR_SUCCESS || type != REG_SZ)
57093:     return PR_FALSE;
62477:   if (aBuffer)
62477:     aBuffer[aBufferLength / sizeof(*aBuffer) - 1] = 0;
62477:   return PR_TRUE;
62477: }
62477: 
62477: static PRBool
62477: IsObsoleteSynapticsDriver()
62477: {
62477:   PRUnichar buf[40];
62477:   PRBool foundKey = GetRegistryKey(HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE,
62477:                                    L"Software\\Synaptics\\SynTP\\Install",
62477:                                    L"DriverVersion",
62477:                                    buf,
62477:                                    sizeof buf);
62477:   if (!foundKey)
62477:     return PR_FALSE;
57093: 
57093:   int majorVersion = wcstol(buf, NULL, 10);
57093:   return majorVersion < 15;
57093: }
57093: 
62477: static PRBool
62477: IsObsoleteElantechDriver()
62477: {
62477:   PRUnichar buf[40];
62477:   // The driver version is found in one of these two registry keys.
62477:   PRBool foundKey = GetRegistryKey(HKEY_CURRENT_USER,
62477:                                    L"Software\\Elantech\\MainOption",
62477:                                    L"DriverVersion",
62477:                                    buf,
62477:                                    sizeof buf);
62477:   if (!foundKey)
62477:     foundKey = GetRegistryKey(HKEY_CURRENT_USER,
62477:                               L"Software\\Elantech",
62477:                               L"DriverVersion",
62477:                               buf,
62477:                               sizeof buf);
62477: 
62477:   if (!foundKey)
62477:     return PR_FALSE;
62477: 
62477:   // Assume that the major version number can be found just after a space
62477:   // or at the start of the string.
62477:   for (PRUnichar* p = buf; *p; p++) {
62477:     if (*p >= L'0' && *p <= L'9' && (p == buf || *(p - 1) == L' ')) {
62477:       int majorVersion = wcstol(p, NULL, 10);
62478:       // Versions 7 and 8 need the hack.
62478:       if (majorVersion == 7 || majorVersion == 8)
62477:         return PR_TRUE;
62477:     }
62477:   }
62477: 
62477:   return PR_FALSE;
62477: }
62477: 
62477: void nsWindow::InitInputWorkaroundPrefDefaults()
33529: {
57093:   if (HasRegistryKey(HKEY_CURRENT_USER, L"Software\\Lenovo\\TrackPoint")) {
57092:     sDefaultTrackPointHack = PR_TRUE;
57093:   } else if (HasRegistryKey(HKEY_CURRENT_USER, L"Software\\Lenovo\\UltraNav")) {
57093:     sDefaultTrackPointHack = PR_TRUE;
57093:   } else if (HasRegistryKey(HKEY_CURRENT_USER, L"Software\\Alps\\Apoint\\TrackPoint")) {
57093:     sDefaultTrackPointHack = PR_TRUE;
57093:   } else if ((HasRegistryKey(HKEY_CURRENT_USER, L"Software\\Synaptics\\SynTPEnh\\UltraNavUSB") ||
57093:               HasRegistryKey(HKEY_CURRENT_USER, L"Software\\Synaptics\\SynTPEnh\\UltraNavPS2")) &&
57093:               IsObsoleteSynapticsDriver()) {
57093:     sDefaultTrackPointHack = PR_TRUE;
57092:   }
62477: 
62477:   sUseElantechGestureHacks =
62477:     GetInputWorkaroundPref("ui.elantech_gesture_hacks.enabled",
62477:                            IsObsoleteElantechDriver());
33529: }
33529: #endif // #if !defined(WINCE)

30750:   ::ClientToScreen(mWnd, &pt);
30750:   return MAKELPARAM(pt.x, pt.y);
30750: }

29835: // return the style for a child nsWindow
29835: DWORD ChildWindow::WindowStyle()
29835: {
29835:   DWORD style = WS_CLIPCHILDREN | nsWindow::WindowStyle();
29835:   if (!(style & WS_POPUP))
29835:     style |= WS_CHILD; // WS_POPUP and WS_CHILD are mutually exclusive.
29835:   VERIFY_WINDOW_STYLE(style);
29835:   return style;
31006: }
